\subsection{Function Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceENSEM_aee2482527c2e020e327d542d07e92dee}\label{namespaceENSEM_aee2482527c2e020e327d542d07e92dee}} 
\index{ENSEM@{ENSEM}!antiSymTensor@{antiSymTensor}}
\index{antiSymTensor@{antiSymTensor}!ENSEM@{ENSEM}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{antiSymTensor()}{antiSymTensor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$int N$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__defs_ga958dd8b23f0fe048624bd04c42201408}{Tensor\+Real}} E\+N\+S\+E\+M\+::anti\+Sym\+Tensor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Antisymmetric tensor. 

For now, instead of making a struct/tag for special ops like Gamma matrices, make a function that constructs a real Tensor object and simply manually do the contractions using contract

This is not optimal and certainly wasteful, but its quick and easy to get going. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceENSEM_a4ce86ea9e03a33e62daa145e7832fa29}\label{namespaceENSEM_a4ce86ea9e03a33e62daa145e7832fa29}}
